bash-4.4$ cat twitter_data.txt | grep -o '@[A-Za-z0-9_]*' | sort | uniq -c | sort -nr | head -30
cat: twitter_data.txt: No such file or directory
# Again, the file 'twitter_data.txt' is missing, resulting in failure
